      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n32121-5" target="غِفَارَةٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n32112"/></foreign> are names applied to <hi rend="ital">a portion of mail</hi> [<hi rend="ital">forming a headcovering</hi>], which is also called <foreign lang="ar">تَسْبِغَةٌ</foreign> [q. v.]; <hi rend="ital">and sometimes the rings are exposed to view; and sometimes they line them within, and cover them externally, with</hi>
